S   ->   NP VP

PP   ->   P NP | IN NP | ADVP IN NP
ADVP   ->   RB

NP   ->   PRP | NNP | DT NN | NN | QP NNS | QP | CD NN | NP PP | NNP NNPS | NP SBAR | PRP$ JJ NN CC JJ NN NNS

VP   ->   VB | VB NP | VB NP PP | VB PP | V VP | V PP | VBD NP PP | VBZ NP

SBAR   ->   WHADVP S
WHADVP   ->   WRB

NP   ->   DT N | DT JJ CD AP NN | DT CD JJ AP NN

AP   ->   RB JJ | RBR JJR | RBS JJS

QP   ->   RB CD

EX   ->   'there'
TO   ->   'to'
WDT   ->   'that' |  'what' |  'whatever' | 'which' | 'whichever'
WP   ->   'that' |  'what' | 'whatever' | 'whatsoever' | 'which' | 'who' | 'whom' | 'whosoever'
WP$   ->   'whose'
